00725 //============================================================================
00726 //  Enumerated Types
00727 //============================================================================
00728 typedef enum SearchStrategy_enum {
00729     IMAQ_CONSERVATIVE               = 1,           //Instructs the pattern matching algorithm to use the largest possible amount of information from the image at the expense of slowing down the speed of the algorithm.
00730     IMAQ_BALANCED                   = 2,           //Instructs the pattern matching algorithm to balance the amount of information from the image it uses with the speed of the algorithm.
00731     IMAQ_AGGRESSIVE                 = 3,           //Instructs the pattern matching algorithm to use a lower amount of information from the image, which allows the algorithm to run quickly but at the expense of accuracy.
00732     IMAQ_VERY_AGGRESSIVE            = 4,           //Instructs the pattern matching algorithm to use the smallest possible amount of information from the image, which allows the algorithm to run at the highest speed possible but at the expense of accuracy.
00733     IMAQ_SEARCH_STRATEGY_SIZE_GUARD = 0xFFFFFFFF   
00734 } SearchStrategy;
00735 
00736 typedef enum MeterArcMode_enum {
00737     IMAQ_METER_ARC_ROI             = 0,           //The function uses the roi parameter and ignores the base, start, and end parameters.
00738     IMAQ_METER_ARC_POINTS          = 1,           //The function uses the base,start, and end parameters and ignores the roi parameter.
00739     IMAQ_METER_ARC_MODE_SIZE_GUARD = 0xFFFFFFFF   
00740 } MeterArcMode;
00741 
00742 typedef enum MorphologyMethod_enum {
00743     IMAQ_AUTOM                        = 0,           //The function uses a transformation that generates simpler particles that contain fewer details.
00744     IMAQ_CLOSE                        = 1,           //The function uses a transformation that fills tiny holes and smooths boundaries.
00745     IMAQ_DILATE                       = 2,           //The function uses a transformation that eliminates tiny holes isolated in particles and expands the contour of the particles according to the template defined by the structuring element.
00746     IMAQ_ERODE                        = 3,           //The function uses a transformation that eliminates pixels isolated in the background and erodes the contour of particles according to the template defined by the structuring element.
00747     IMAQ_GRADIENT                     = 4,           //The function uses a transformation that leaves only the pixels that would be added by the dilation process or eliminated by the erosion process.
00748     IMAQ_GRADIENTOUT                  = 5,           //The function uses a transformation that leaves only the pixels that would be added by the dilation process.
00749     IMAQ_GRADIENTIN                   = 6,           //The function uses a transformation that leaves only the pixels that would be eliminated by the erosion process.
00750     IMAQ_HITMISS                      = 7,           //The function uses a transformation that extracts each pixel located in a neighborhood exactly matching the template defined by the structuring element.
00751     IMAQ_OPEN                         = 8,           //The function uses a transformation that removes small particles and smooths boundaries.
00752     IMAQ_PCLOSE                       = 9,           //The function uses a transformation that fills tiny holes and smooths the inner contour of particles according to the template defined by the structuring element.
00753     IMAQ_POPEN                        = 10,          //The function uses a transformation that removes small particles and smooths the contour of particles according to the template defined by the structuring element.

01429     IMAQ_QR_DEMODULATION_MODE_ALL            = 3,           //The function tries IMAQ_QR_DEMODULATION_MODE_HISTOGRAM, then IMAQ_QR_DEMODULATION_MODE_LOCAL_CONTRAST and then IMAQ_QR_DEMODULATION_MODE_COMBINED, stopping once one mode is successful.
01430     IMAQ_QR_DEMODULATION_MODE_SIZE_GUARD     = 0xFFFFFFFF   
01431 } QRDemodulationMode;

01706     IMAQ_MT_PERIMETER                           = 19,          //Length of the outer boundary of the particle.
01707     IMAQ_MT_CONVEX_HULL_PERIMETER               = 20,          //Perimeter of the smallest convex polygon containing all points in the particle.
01708     IMAQ_MT_HOLES_PERIMETER                     = 21,          //Sum of the perimeters of each hole in the particle.
01709     IMAQ_MT_MAX_FERET_DIAMETER                  = 22,          //Distance between the start and end of the line segment connecting the two perimeter points that are the furthest apart.
01710     IMAQ_MT_EQUIVALENT_ELLIPSE_MAJOR_AXIS       = 23,          //Length of the major axis of the ellipse with the same perimeter and area as the particle.
01711     IMAQ_MT_EQUIVALENT_ELLIPSE_MINOR_AXIS       = 24,          //Length of the minor axis of the ellipse with the same perimeter and area as the particle.
01712     IMAQ_MT_EQUIVALENT_ELLIPSE_MINOR_AXIS_FERET = 25,          //Length of the minor axis of the ellipse with the same area as the particle, and Major Axis equal in length to the Max Feret Diameter.
01713     IMAQ_MT_EQUIVALENT_RECT_LONG_SIDE           = 26,          //Longest side of the rectangle with the same perimeter and area as the particle.
01714     IMAQ_MT_EQUIVALENT_RECT_SHORT_SIDE          = 27,          //Shortest side of the rectangle with the same perimeter and area as the particle.
01715     IMAQ_MT_EQUIVALENT_RECT_DIAGONAL            = 28,          //Distance between opposite corners of the rectangle with the same perimeter and area as the particle.
01716     IMAQ_MT_EQUIVALENT_RECT_SHORT_SIDE_FERET    = 29,          //Shortest side of the rectangle with the same area as the particle, and longest side equal in length to the Max Feret Diameter.
01717     IMAQ_MT_AVERAGE_HORIZ_SEGMENT_LENGTH        = 30,          //Average length of a horizontal segment in the particle.
01718     IMAQ_MT_AVERAGE_VERT_SEGMENT_LENGTH         = 31,          //Average length of a vertical segment in the particle.
01719     IMAQ_MT_HYDRAULIC_RADIUS                    = 32,          //The particle area divided by the particle perimeter.
01720     IMAQ_MT_WADDEL_DISK_DIAMETER                = 33,          //Diameter of a disk with the same area as the particle.
01721     IMAQ_MT_AREA                                = 35,          //Area of the particle.
01722     IMAQ_MT_HOLES_AREA                          = 36,          //Sum of the areas of each hole in the particle.
01723     IMAQ_MT_PARTICLE_AND_HOLES_AREA             = 37,          //Area of a particle that completely covers the image.
01724     IMAQ_MT_CONVEX_HULL_AREA                    = 38,          //Area of the smallest convex polygon containing all points in the particle.
01725     IMAQ_MT_IMAGE_AREA                          = 39,          //Area of the image.
01726     IMAQ_MT_NUMBER_OF_HOLES                     = 41,          //Number of holes in the particle.
01727     IMAQ_MT_NUMBER_OF_HORIZ_SEGMENTS            = 42,          //Number of horizontal segments in the particle.
01728     IMAQ_MT_NUMBER_OF_VERT_SEGMENTS             = 43,          //Number of vertical segments in the particle.
01729     IMAQ_MT_ORIENTATION                         = 45,          //The angle of the line that passes through the particle Center of Mass about which the particle has the lowest moment of inertia.
01730     IMAQ_MT_MAX_FERET_DIAMETER_ORIENTATION      = 46,          //The angle of the line segment connecting the two perimeter points that are the furthest apart.
01731     IMAQ_MT_AREA_BY_IMAGE_AREA                  = 48,          //Percentage of the particle Area covering the Image Area.
01732     IMAQ_MT_AREA_BY_PARTICLE_AND_HOLES_AREA     = 49,          //Percentage of the particle Area in relation to its Particle and Holes Area.
01733     IMAQ_MT_RATIO_OF_EQUIVALENT_ELLIPSE_AXES    = 50,          //Equivalent Ellipse Major Axis divided by Equivalent Ellipse Minor Axis.
01734     IMAQ_MT_RATIO_OF_EQUIVALENT_RECT_SIDES      = 51,          //Equivalent Rect Long Side divided by Equivalent Rect Short Side.
01735     IMAQ_MT_ELONGATION_FACTOR                   = 53,          //Max Feret Diameter divided by Equivalent Rect Short Side (Feret).
01736     IMAQ_MT_COMPACTNESS_FACTOR                  = 54,          //Area divided by the product of Bounding Rect Width and Bounding Rect Height.
01737     IMAQ_MT_HEYWOOD_CIRCULARITY_FACTOR          = 55,          //Perimeter divided by the circumference of a circle with the same area.
01738     IMAQ_MT_TYPE_FACTOR                         = 56,          //Factor relating area to moment of inertia.
01739     IMAQ_MT_SUM_X                               = 58,          //The sum of all x-coordinates in the particle.
01740     IMAQ_MT_SUM_Y                               = 59,          //The sum of all y-coordinates in the particle.
01741     IMAQ_MT_SUM_XX                              = 60,          //The sum of all x-coordinates squared in the particle.
01742     IMAQ_MT_SUM_XY                              = 61,          //The sum of all x-coordinates times y-coordinates in the particle.
01743     IMAQ_MT_SUM_YY                              = 62,          //The sum of all y-coordinates squared in the particle.
01744     IMAQ_MT_SUM_XXX                             = 63,          //The sum of all x-coordinates cubed in the particle.
01745     IMAQ_MT_SUM_XXY                             = 64,          //The sum of all x-coordinates squared times y-coordinates in the particle.
01746     IMAQ_MT_SUM_XYY                             = 65,          //The sum of all x-coordinates times y-coordinates squared in the particle.
01747     IMAQ_MT_SUM_YYY                             = 66,          //The sum of all y-coordinates cubed in the particle.
01748     IMAQ_MT_MOMENT_OF_INERTIA_XX                = 68,          //The moment of inertia in the x-direction twice.
01749     IMAQ_MT_MOMENT_OF_INERTIA_XY                = 69,          //The moment of inertia in the x and y directions.
01750     IMAQ_MT_MOMENT_OF_INERTIA_YY                = 70,          //The moment of inertia in the y-direction twice.
01751     IMAQ_MT_MOMENT_OF_INERTIA_XXX               = 71,          //The moment of inertia in the x-direction three times.
01752     IMAQ_MT_MOMENT_OF_INERTIA_XXY               = 72,          //The moment of inertia in the x-direction twice and the y-direction once.
01753     IMAQ_MT_MOMENT_OF_INERTIA_XYY               = 73,          //The moment of inertia in the x-direction once and the y-direction twice.
01754     IMAQ_MT_MOMENT_OF_INERTIA_YYY               = 74,          //The moment of inertia in the y-direction three times.
01755     IMAQ_MT_NORM_MOMENT_OF_INERTIA_XX           = 75,          //The normalized moment of inertia in the x-direction twice.
01756     IMAQ_MT_NORM_MOMENT_OF_INERTIA_XY           = 76,          //The normalized moment of inertia in the x- and y-directions.
01757     IMAQ_MT_NORM_MOMENT_OF_INERTIA_YY           = 77,          //The normalized moment of inertia in the y-direction twice.
01758     IMAQ_MT_NORM_MOMENT_OF_INERTIA_XXX          = 78,          //The normalized moment of inertia in the x-direction three times.
01759     IMAQ_MT_NORM_MOMENT_OF_INERTIA_XXY          = 79,          //The normalized moment of inertia in the x-direction twice and the y-direction once.

01761     IMAQ_MT_NORM_MOMENT_OF_INERTIA_YYY          = 81,          //The normalized moment of inertia in the y-direction three times.

02454     unsigned int               rows;                 //The number of rows in the Data Matrix barcode.
02455     unsigned int               columns;              //The number of columns in the Data Matrix barcode.
02456     DataMatrixECC              ecc;                  //The Error Correction Code (ECC) used by the Data Matrix barcode.

03722     int showRotatedRectangleTool; //If TRUE, the rotated rectangle tool becomes visible.
03723     int showPanTool;              //If TRUE, the pan tool becomes visible.
03724     int reserved1;                //This element is reserved and should be set to FALSE.
03725     int reserved2;                //This element is reserved and should be set to FALSE.
03726     int reserved3;                //This element is reserved and should be set to FALSE.
03727     int reserved4;                //This element is reserved and should be set to FALSE.
03728 } ToolWindowOptions;
03729 
03730 typedef struct SpokeOptions_struct {
03731     int                 threshold;         //Specifies the threshold value for the contrast of the edge.
03732     int                 width;             //The number of pixels that the function averages to find the contrast at either side of the edge.
03733     int                 steepness;         //The span, in pixels, of the slope of the edge projected along the path specified by the input points.
03734     double              subsamplingRatio;  //The angle, in degrees, between each radial search line in the spoke.
03735     InterpolationMethod subpixelType;      //The method for interpolating.
03736     int                 subpixelDivisions; //The number of samples the function obtains from a pixel.
03737 } SpokeOptions;
